*********************************************************************** 00020000
*                                                                     * 00030000
*  MACRO NAME:     /DISPLAY OUTPUT DSECTS                             * 00040000
*                                                                     * 00050000
*  STATUS:         IMS 12.1                                           * 00060000
*                                                                     * 00070000
*  FUNCTION:       DISPLAY DSECTS THAT MAP THE DISPLAY OUTPUT LINE    * 00080000
*                  FOR /DISPLAY COMMANDS.  ALL DISPLAY LINES MUST     * 00090000
*                  END WITH A X'15' NEWLINE CHARACTER.  HEADER LINES  * 00100000
*                  MUST HAVE AN ADDITIONAL NEWLINE CHARACTER AFTER    * 00110000
*                  THE LLZZ OF THE DISPLAY LINE.  THE CONVENTION      * 00120000
*                  FOR NUMBERING DISPLAY DSECT LINES FOLLOWS:         * 00130000
*                                                                     * 00140000
*                  X00-X49:  DISPLAY BODY LINE                        * 00150000
*                  X50-X69:  DISPLAY ERROR MESSAGE LINE               * 00160000
*                  X70-X79:  DISPLAY HEADER LINE                      * 00170000
*                                                                     * 00180000
*  EXAMPLE:        DISPLAY TYPE=B WILL EXPAND ALL OF THE DISPLAY      * 00190000
*                  DSECTS THAT BEGIN WITH B.                          * 00200000
*                                                                     * 00210000
* 05/01/03  ARS  UP9C01AS  V9R1  Forward fit to 9C                    * 00220000
* 03/12/07  mnz  PK42601   V101  /DIS AFFIN for MSC VGR               * 00230000
* 05/10/08  djr  PK70078   V10D  /DIS ACTIVE REG WAIT-CALLOUT         * 00240000
* 06/28/08  JR   PK70078   V10D  /DIS TMEM TPIPE SYNC                 * 00250000
* 07/31/08  djr  PK70078   V10D  /DIS ACTIVE REG TPIPE: tpipe         * 00260000
* 08/15/08  AV   PK68223   V101  CHANGE ELEM/ENTRY RATIO TO 5 DIGITS  * 00270000
* 10/09/08  djr  KB20029   V11A  FF of PK70078 & PK73539 to V11       * 00280000
* 03/30/09  JR   PK81543   V111  FF OF PK71135                        * 00290000
* 12/08/09  mnz  PM03085   V11   Remove TCP/IP NAME HDRS - FF PK85347 * 00300000
* 04/15/10  JCY  PM12142   V11   Display OTMA ICAL count      PM12142 * 00310000
* 04/15/10  SSC  PM05424   V11   ADD WID KEYWORD                      * 00320000
*--------------------------V12.1--------------------------------------* 00330000
* 02/19/09  SSC  UP12A1SC  V12A  CORRECT A67LEN                       * 00340000
* 07/15/09  jcy  U12VJY1   V121  Add ACEEAGE to /DIS OTMA             * 00350000
* 06/30/09  KQN  U12RKN1   V12R  /DIS OTMA, /DIS APPC AND /DIS ACTIVE * 00360000
* 04/30/10  KQN  KC30234   V12R  REMOVE OTMA IO TIMEOUT               * 00370000

* 10/28/11  BRM  PM33681   V12   Show tpipe count /DIS OTMA & TMEMBER * 00420000
*--------------------------V13.1--------------------------------------* 00430000

*                                                                       88840000
*  DCL                                                                  88850000
*    XACTIVE  CHAR(6)   CONSTANT('ACTIVE'); /* 'ACTIVE'              */ 88860000
*  DCL                                                                  88870000
*    XBACKUP  CHAR(6)   CONSTANT('BACKUP'); /* 'BACKUP'              */ 88880000
*  DCL                                                                  88890000
*    XBLANK   CHAR(1)   CONSTANT(' '); /* blank                      */ 88900000
